docs/architecture_decision_records/016-universal-model-architecture.md:* **Description:** Train a **Single Universal Model** for all substations and all horizons. The model is trained on a "long-format" dataset. It explicitly receives `lead_time_hours` as a feature to learn how weather sensitivity decays over time, and `substation_number` as a categorical feature to learn spatial differences. It also natively supports ensemble NWP inputs by passing each ensemble member through the model to generate a distribution of power forecasts.
